Investigation of the Japanese Army's Invasion of Northeast Troops

Five Divisions and Three Independent Brigades

Tianjin Special Dispatch: Since the September 18th Incident, the four northeastern provinces have successively fallen. However, the Japanese military strength is no more than five divisions and three independent mixed brigades, totaling no more than 80,000 to 90,000 people. We, on the other hand, mobilized a large number of troops, no less than 300,000 to 400,000 people. The bloody resistance at various passes of the Great Wall can demonstrate the spirit of our soldiers in resisting aggression. The reason for the failure is the lack of a complete line of resistance, resulting in inaction at the tail when striking the head, and inaction at the head when striking the tail. This is the biggest reason for the failure. Secondly, our weapons are inferior to those of the enemy. According to a certain important person, apart from airplanes and tanks being unique to the enemy, our guns and artillery are also inferior in comparison. Often, the enemy has ten machine guns, while we only have four. The enemy has ten artillery pieces, while we only have two. The enemy's transportation is by car, while ours is by mule cart. The enemy's ammunition is replenished by air, while ours is replenished by manpower. This is another reason for the failure. Now, an investigation table of the Japanese army's invading Northeast troops is recorded on the left:

Commander of the Kwantung Army: Muto Nobuyoshi; Chief of Staff: Isoya Kuniaki; Deputy Chief of Staff: Okamura Yasuji, all stationed in Changchun.

6th Infantry Division (Kumamoto): Commander: Sakamoto Masayoshi, stationed in Lingyuan; Chief of Staff: Sasaki Yoshira, stationed in Pingquan; 11th Brigade Command stationed between Lingyuan and Lengkou, Brigade Commander: Matsuda Kunizo; 13th Regiment: Washizu Enpei; 47th Regiment: Tsunekawa Kanji; 36th Brigade Command stationed in Weichang, Brigade Commander: Takada Mina; 23rd Regiment: Shido Hoyasu, stationed in Bianqiangshan; 45th Regiment: Mukai Senhachi, stationed in Lengkou; 6th Cavalry Regiment: Koda Kikuo; 6th Field Artillery Regiment: Shirojima Eiko; 6th Engineer Battalion: Hosome Shiro; 6th Transport Battalion: Kushima Isoji.

When the division began to attack Rehe, the Matsuda Brigade first coordinated with the Suzuki Brigade to occupy Chaoyang. Then, the Matsuda Brigade was dispatched as the left column, the Koda Cavalry as the central column, and the Takada Brigade as the right column, departing from Chaoyang, Zhangwu, and Tongliao, respectively, and committing westward offenses in multiple routes. The Shido Detachment and the Mogi Cavalry Brigade were also dispatched to cooperate, passing through Xiawa and Chifeng to reach Weichang directly. The Matsuda Brigade followed the movement of the 8th Division as a reserve force. In mid-March, the Takada section of Kailu Chifeng and the Matsuda Brigade gradually moved south toward the Great Wall line. In late March, the Mukai Detachment under Takada engaged in fierce battles with our army at Lengkou.

8th Infantry Division (Hirosaki): Commander: Nishi Yoshiichi, stationed in Chengde; Chief of Staff: Shuno Seiichi; 4th Brigade Command in Chengde, Brigade Commander: Suzuki Mitsuru; 5th Regiment: Tani Giichi; 31st Regiment: Hayakawa Tomaru; 16th Brigade Command in Gubeikou, Brigade Commander: Kawahara Kanji; 17th Regiment: Nagase Takehei; 32nd Regiment: Sato Masaburo; 3rd Cavalry Brigade, Brigade Commander: Iida Sadakoto; 8th Regiment: Miyake Tadashi; 23rd Regiment: Tamura Yasaburo; 24th Regiment: Ashimi Shigeru; 8th Field Artillery Regiment: Chikawa Hajime; 8th Engineer Battalion: Uehara Kenichi; 8th Transport Battalion: Nakamura Sadaharu.

Subsequently, the Nagase Detachment advanced towards Gubeikou, while the Hayakawa Detachment (from Chaoyang) and the Tani Detachment (from Mingshuitangmen) continued to arrive at Pingquan and Chengde. The Kawahara Brigade and the Miyake Cavalry Brigade then launched a full-scale attack on our Gubeikou. On March 9th, the brigade was heavily attacked by us and was on the verge of collapse. Division Commander Nishi Yoshiichi personally went to Gubeikou to supervise the battle, and the Ogura Field Heavy Artillery Corps was added to the front line for support. The Suzuki Brigade used the Hayakawa Detachment to depart from Chengde on March 13th and attack our Luowenyu. In late March, the Miyake Cavalry Brigade coordinated with infantry and advanced further to attack Fengning.

10th Infantry Division (Himeji): Commander: Hirose Hisasuke; Chief of Staff: Kano Toyohisa; 8th Brigade Commander: Ranbe KazuiIchiro; 39th Regiment: Funahashi Shigeru; 40th Regiment: Okamura Gen; 33rd Brigade Command in the area of Lengkou Jielingkou Yiyuankou, Brigade Commander: Nakamura Kaoru; 10th Regiment: Hitomi Shunji; 63rd Regiment: Nakamura Otoichi; 10th Cavalry Regiment: Matsuda Jinzaburo; 10th Field Artillery Regiment: Taniguchi Motojiro; 10th Engineer Battalion: Tanaka Ryosaku; 10th Transport Battalion: Hattori Uzaburo.

(April 29)

Bloody Battle of Nantianmen

Talks with Company Commander Lin of the Huang Division

Japanese Army Relying on Artillery Barrage

Our Officers and Soldiers Advanced in the Face of Bullets

Shixia Communication: Since the enemy army began attacking our Nantianmen position on the morning of April 21st, our brave officers and soldiers have fought bloody battles for several days. Thousands of national heroes have completed their mission and returned to paradise. The enemy has paid an extremely high price and still cannot gain an inch of land in Nantianmen. Now they are urgently mobilizing reinforcements, plotting to launch another attack. It is expected that there will be a more intense war in the near future. The following is a detailed record of the battles of the past few days, according to Company Commander Lin of Huang Jie's unit:

On the 21st, just as the morning light was dawning, six or seven enemy planes suddenly appeared in the air above our position, circling up and down. The enemy artillery took them as targets and concentrated their fire for a fierce barrage. At the same time, more than 2,000 Mongolian and puppet soldiers also attacked our Nantianmen and Badaolouzi area under the cover of their artillery fire. Their target was particularly focused on the left-wing Badaolouzi position, which was higher than Nantianmen and extremely dangerous. At this time, only one battalion of our defending soldiers was stationed here. After several hours of fighting, the position had been leveled by bombardment, and casualties were more than half. However, our officers and soldiers were all calm and resisted the enemy. Even if they died until the last person, they would not retreat. Those who were injured and fell to the ground still struggled to crawl forward until they fell to their deaths. A certain platoon leader was injured and replaced by a sergeant. The entire platoon was surrounded by Japanese soldiers and fought for three days and nights. They still led more than 20 people to break through the encirclement and return to the camp to report. The bravery of our officers and soldiers and their determination to die for the country can be seen from this. However, the battalion has almost all been killed or wounded. As a result, Badaolouzi was once captured by the enemy. Although our reinforcements had rushed to the scene, they had to temporarily hold the nearby high ground because the enemy's artillery fire was too fierce. That night at 8 o'clock, Division Commander Huang Jie took advantage of the darkness and ordered a counterattack. Our loyal and brave officers and soldiers advanced in the face of bullets. The enemy still drove the Mongolian and puppet soldiers in front and supervised the battle from behind with machine guns and artillery. When the puppet soldiers came into contact with our army, the Japanese army concentrated its firepower on the battle line, regardless of friend or foe. Their intention was not only to eliminate our army, but also to eliminate the puppet army in one fell swoop. From this, we can see the cunning of the Japanese pirates and the pitifulness and hatred of the puppet army. Although our army suffered many casualties in this battle, the enemy suffered even more than us. After a night of hard fighting, the Badaolouzi position was finally recovered by our army. On the 22nd, the enemy sent more than a thousand people to detour to our left wing. The situation was very critical. Division Commander Huang personally led the entire 8th Regiment to run forward and meet them head-on. The enemy's plan failed again. Our army took advantage of this opportunity to launch a rapid attack. The smoke was misty and the screams shook the field. The enemy army was panicked and suffered heavy losses. On the 24th, the enemy launched an attack on us with even greater force, with thousands of Mongolian, puppet, and Japanese soldiers divided into several routes. The battle was even more tragic. However, our officers and soldiers still adhered to their patriotic enthusiasm and vowed to coexist with the position. It is still not possible to estimate how much more the Japanese will sacrifice to seize our Nantianmen position.

In this battle, the enemy's artillery fire played the greatest role. In Badaolouzi alone, more than 3,000 shells landed. Not only was the battlefield leveled, but even the stones were pulverized. Therefore, our sacrifices were extremely large. Two battalion commanders were killed and three were injured. More than 2,000 officers and soldiers were injured. The enemy, on the other hand, took the offensive and suffered even more casualties than us. Furthermore, the power of the enemy's aircraft in this battle was very weak and not worth fearing. When our Division Commander Huang led the entire regiment to run forward to meet the enemy detouring to our left wing, dozens of enemy planes followed and dropped bombs, but our army did not suffer any casualties. (April 28)

Reorganization of the Beiping Political Council

Chen Gongbo Comes North to Negotiate the Rate

Number of Committee Members Larger Than Before

Beiping Special Dispatch: The politics of the northern provinces have always held a special status due to historical and geographical factors. After the success of the Northern Expedition of the Kuomintang, the Beiping Political Affairs Branch was established to manage everything as a transition mechanism between the central government and local areas. Zhang Ji was the chairman. Later, all political affairs branches across the country were abolished, and the council was dissolved. In the nineteenth year, Zhang Xueliang led his troops into the customs and established the Deputy Commander's Headquarters in addition to setting up political and military affairs committees to discuss military and political matters. This institution was not legally created by the central government, and its powers were limited. As the political situation evolved, the Deputy Commander's Headquarters became the Beiping Pacification Headquarters, and then the Beiping Branch of the Military Affairs Committee of the National Government. The original Military Affairs Committee was changed to the Military Training Committee due to a conflict in name. The Beiping Political Affairs Committee remained as before. Until Zhang Xueliang stepped down, the military affairs were managed by He Yingqin, who was sent by the central government. In terms of politics, it was also necessary to reorganize under a unified standard. The Central Political Committee recently decided to abolish the Beiping Political Affairs Committee and set up a legitimate institution. The central government, in order to be cautious due to the complexity of the political situation in the north and the special nature of the local areas, specially sent Chen Gongbo to the north to exchange opinions with various parties to avoid any obstacles. After arriving in Ping, Chen consulted with He Yingqin, Huang Shaohong, Jiang Bocheng, and others, and exchanged opinions with important figures in Pingjin. It is said that there have been considerable results. Generally, a political affairs institution will still be established in Ping. As for the name, the name of the former political affairs branch was explicitly abolished by the central government and is not suitable for re-mention. Most people advocate still calling it the Political Affairs Committee. In terms of organization, some advocate changing to a standing committee system, and some advocate setting up a chairman. After consultation, most people still think it is more convenient to set up a chairman. As for the number of committee members, I still remember that at the beginning of the establishment of the Beiping Political Affairs Committee, there were eleven committee members, and Zhang Xueliang also served as the chairman. Later, Wang Yitang, Shi Yousan, Gu Zhongxiu, and others were hired as committee members, which resulted in fifteen people. In this reorganization, most people suggest slightly expanding the number of committee members, and all important figures from various factions should be recruited. It is said that Wang Yitang of the Duan faction, Zhang Zhitan of the Zhili faction, Liu Zhe and Wang Shuhan, important figures in the Northeast, Xiong Xiling, a famous figure, Wu Dingchang and Zhou Zuomin from the banking industry, are all on the list of recruits. Several people from the central government will participate, and the northern power factions will also recommend several people. The total number should be more than twenty. There is a saying that one of Zhang Ji, Li Shizeng, Huang Shaohong, and Huang Fu will be selected for the post of chairman, which can be announced after Chen Gongbo returns to Beijing for consultation.

The Military Affairs Committee was originally established to connect the feelings of the various armies, but since it was changed to the Military Training Committee, it has become nominal. Now that the northern military and political affairs are being reorganized, the committee has been ordered to be abolished. Yesterday, the committee removed the plaque in front of the door, and all places were completely closed. (April 29)

Efforts to Work Situation

More Than Ten Rescue Teams

More Than Twenty Shelters

Ping News: Since the outbreak of the war in Yu-Rehe, the Beiping General Assembly of the Red Swastika Society has organized nine major rescue teams stationed in Feng, Nantianmen, Gubeikou, Miyun, Shixia, Lengkou, Duolun, Zhangjiakou, Luanxian, Tangshan, and other places to rescue wounded soldiers and refugees. Main Bandit Forces Gather in the Upper Reaches of the Fu River

Create One Million Steel Red Army

Nanchang Communication: The 135th Army Corps, one of the main forces of the pseudo-First Front Army, is currently gathered in Fenggang, in the Yihuang, Le'an, and Chongren border area in the upper reaches of the Fu River. Zhu and Mao are traveling back and forth to recruit and command the Shuinan Dongbei Huangbei area. In recent days, the main bandit forces have launched attacks on Yihuang Chongren in several routes, and scattered bandits have sneaked into the territory of Linchuan to disrupt traffic in plainclothes and plan to invade Fuzhou. The content is as follows: (1) Create one million steel Red Army in all Soviet areas in China to fight against the imperialist Kuomintang army. The Gan and Min provinces must transport 10,000 new soldiers to the front in one month. Workers and peasants save one copper coin every day to purchase airplanes and military aircraft. (5) The Provincial Committees of Jiangxi and Fujian should make their greatest efforts to immediately strengthen leadership over newly developed areas, such as Ningdu, Guangchang, Yihuang, Le'an, Nanfeng, Lichuan, and Shicheng in Jiangxi, and Jianning, Taining, Ninghua, Liancheng, Guihua, and Qingwan in Fujian.

The Central Bank's 159th Issuance Reserve Inspection Report states: In accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Law, this council is responsible for inspecting the reserve funds for the issuance of convertible banknotes by the Central Bank. The 159th inspection was conducted at the Issuance Bureau of the Central Bank on April 30, 1933. The results of the inspection are hereby announced as follows: (A) Total issuance of convertible banknotes: 44,468,5919 silver dollars, including: 40,425,149 silver dollar notes and 4,260,770 converted currency notes. Total convertible banknote reserve: 44,468,5919 silver dollars, including: 36,886,919 silver dollars in cash reserve. This cash reserve includes 31,982,979 silver dollars stored in the bank's issuing vault, 3,100,0919 silver dollars stored in branches in various ports, and 1,800,3021 silver dollars stored in correspondent banks. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 7,799,000 silver dollars. (B) Total issuance of customs gold convertible banknotes: 417,269.4 yuan. Total customs gold convertible banknote reserve: 417,269.4 yuan. This reserve includes 7,004.69 taels of standard gold, which is converted to 417,269.4 yuan of customs gold at the fixed price of 0.5957. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's Convertible Banknote Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The inspection results show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the guarantee reserve is less than 40%, which is in compliance with the regulations. This report is hereby made. April 30, 1933. Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank: Li Fusun, Supervisors: Wang Jingli, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Qia Qing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Ji.

The content is divided into five parts: The first part, "The World in Distress," describes the Far Eastern problem, which is filled with gunpowder smoke and is enough to cause a world war; the independence movements of Near Eastern countries such as the Philippines, India, Turkey, Persia, and Afghanistan; the European situation dancing on a powder keg; and the countries in various revolutionary upheavals. Reader's Advisor

The Trend of Future World Wars

丨Letter from Mr. Lu Sheng of this city丨

Dear Reporter: Since the Nazi Party came to power in Germany, it has strongly suppressed the open activities of the Communist Party on the one hand, and actively confronted France on the other. The European political situation has suddenly become extremely tense. As a result, the British Prime Minister personally visited Italy, ostensibly under the guise of a new disarmament conference, but in reality to discuss general important issues. Subsequently, the talks between the British and Italian Prime Ministers resulted in the cooperation of the four major European powers.

Originally, our observation of the world political situation in the past ten days was just as Mr. Nai in the Shen Bao's commentary said: "The mode of the Second World War will be a conflict between imperialist powers, rather than a united struggle of imperialist powers against the Soviet Union." However, the eve of the outbreak of war is precisely the time when the political situation changes most rapidly. My opinion is that the mode of the Second World War cannot be definitively determined to be a conflict between imperialist powers; in other words, the crisis of the imperialist powers jointly attacking the Soviet Union has not diminished slightly. Not only has it not diminished, but it has become increasingly acute. The best example is the recent incident in which the Soviet Union dealt with British engineers, which aroused a strong reaction from the British authorities; and the severe suppression of the Communist Party by the Italian and German Fascist parties, followed by the Soviet Union's protest against Hitler; and a few days ago, Japanese nationalists allowed White Russians to have political organizations at the border between the so-called "Manchurian" and Soviet countries; moreover, the leader of the anti-Soviet Union movement in Western Europe has shifted from France to the hands of the British Empire, and the person visited by the British Prime Minister this time is precisely Mussolini. What is the result of their talks? How to make the four major European powers cooperate? Since we know that the imperialist powers cannot cooperate due to conflicts of interest, does Mussolini not know this? The truth of the matter is that when the conflicts between the imperialist powers become acute, there is often some non-war treaty or some peace conference. On the one hand, it is to seek a temporary easing of the atmosphere between the imperialist powers, and at the same time, cooperation is only sought when attacking a common enemy. The European four-power cooperation advocated by Mussolini is nothing more than to ease the tense atmosphere between the four powers, and on the other hand, to actively unite to attack their common enemy - the Soviet Union!

Dear Reporter, because I cannot directly discuss this issue with Mr. Nai, I am writing a few words to ask you to reply to my opinion, what do you think?

Answer: Your letter disagrees with the Shen Bao Naijun's March 20th commentary on the world war situation [The mode of the Second World War will be a conflict between imperialist powers rather than a united struggle of imperialist powers against the Soviet Union.]'s assessment, arguing that "the crisis of the imperialist powers jointly attacking the Soviet Union has not diminished slightly." This issue is very serious, and the Chinese people have different ideas about these two arguments, that is, each has its own illusions. If we do not discuss in detail, recognize the future of international situation development, and determine the attitude that we Chinese people should take and the preparations for the major changes in the future, then it is really very dangerous. It should be solemnly raised and readers should pay full attention to it and discuss it carefully. This reporter is foolish to think that the discussion of this issue should not be based solely on a certain isolated matter, a certain diplomatic event, or a formal change in the international arena, but should pay attention to the following facts: (1) From the perspective of the class instinct of international imperialists, they are always trying to attack the Soviet Union, because there is something that can kill them "next to the bed", that is, the world has the other new thing of the Soviet Union's socialist federation, which is always enough to arouse the suspicion of the world's general public about the old society (capitalist society) and to strike at the imperialist powers; (2) Jointly attacking the Soviet Union and eliminating the socialist federation, this war, Japan in the East, Germany in the West (Hitler's Germany), and even Britain, France, and the United States, do not oppose it in principle. For the time being, they can ease their own conflicts, and Hitler uses this as an exchange condition for demanding equal armaments and restoring pre-war colonies; Japan uses this as a way to annex our Northeast and take advantage of this to seize Siberia and the coastal provinces, incorporating them into its own territory, which is indeed a good plan; (3) However, they are not fools. The current Soviet Union is at least not the Soviet Union of 1918-1922. The countries at that time did not benefit from entering politics. Now, to attack, at least prepare several times the previous strength and several times the previous sacrifices. Perhaps Hitler's Germany and Araki's Japan will be the vanguard in the future, but how will the result be, there is no guarantee. Although the German revolutionaries are temporarily oppressed by the violence of the Brownshirts, from the streets to the basements, if a war with the Soviet Union breaks out, they will come out of the basements again, run to the streets, pick up weapons, and disrupt Hitler's camp. Japan has just completed the conquest of China, but how to appease the opposition, how to develop industry, how to actively prepare, and how to cope with the situation in the Pacific, he does not dare to act rashly; (4) Japan's occupation of the three northeastern provinces and Jehol is naturally with the tacit consent of the great powers such as Britain, France, and Italy; France uses it to restrain Soviet Russia, Britain uses it to restrain his strong enemy the United States, Italy has very little relationship with the East, and has no real power to intervene externally, so it has to listen to it. The most threatened here are the United States and Soviet Russia: the Soviet Union is closing its doors to do its second five-year plan, trying its best to tolerate it, and although the United States knows it, if he wants to maintain the future of his capital, he can only interfere in Japan's monopoly of China with force, but if his military power does not cooperate with the Soviet Union or Britain, he will have no choice but to deal with Japan. Moreover, his own crisis is full of loopholes, "war is often the yeast of revolution," he knows this, and Britain and Japan also know this. Therefore, in this critical period, they are always trying to avoid armed conflict; (5) But although they are running around and shouting, trying their best to avoid conflict, on the one hand, it also proves that the explosiveness of their conflict is increasing extremely, and the poisonous beard of war has touched their consciousness. Therefore, their preparations for war are becoming more active and harder. Then, when everyone is at daggers drawn and the gunpowder is set, as long as someone pulls the fuse, like the blow of Archduke Ferdinand, it will immediately erupt; (6) When we assess the international situation, we must not forget the national movements in the colonies, such as the Sino-Japanese problem. After Japan's imperialists have realized the first step of their plan to invade the four northeastern provinces, of course they have to stop for a while to reorganize the land they have acquired. In China, they are only saying "if the enemy attacks, we will definitely resist". The implication, is it not exactly to the Japanese imperialists' liking? However, the main reason for the demise of the former Qing government was diplomatic failure, ceding land and seeking peace. Today's view of the past is exactly the same. China's national movement will never subside as they wishfully fantasize. China's national movement will definitely continue to develop, increasing the explosiveness and speed of world war. Therefore, in terms of the class position and fundamental interests of capitalist imperialists, attacking the Soviet Union is naturally more beneficial than fighting each other; however, whether their own conflicts of interest can be completely consistent is a question. The attitude of France and the small Entente countries he leads towards the so-called four-power cooperation shows this; that is, for the United States to attack the Soviet Union, based on his current interests, he gains very little, and naturally he is not very enthusiastic. No matter which aspect you look at this issue, I think it is a bit dangerous to draw a definite conclusion suddenly. At least I personally do not have this courage. As for Naijun's opinion that "the French feel the danger between their elbows, so they have to...conclude a non-aggression treaty with the Soviet Union. The so-called anti-Soviet front has disappeared," I am afraid it is also too optimistic. We should of course not forget "the conflict between imperialisms," that is, the internal contradictions of international capitalism, but at the same time, we must not forget the sharp conflict between the two major camps internationally. As for whether the recent international conflict will be an attack on the Soviet Union or a conflict between imperialists, it depends on how the aforementioned situation develops. This is this reporter's personal opinion, and I ask everyone to discuss it.

Lecture at the Ministry of Education's Memorial Week

"Rationalizing Chinese Education Research"

丨Lecture by Li Jiaxiang, European Inspection Commissioner丨

On the morning of May 1st, when the Ministry of Education held the Memorial Week, it invited Li Jiaxiang, European Education Inspection Commissioner, to give a lecture. Li spoke on "Rationalizing Chinese Education Research," stating that since China's self-government, internal and external troubles have been frequent, and the people's strength has been scattered and inconsistent. To save its ills, it depends on education. At the time of national crisis, it is especially important to find a way out from education. In the past, Chinese education lacked a center for collective research. Those who returned from studying abroad established their own schools, and there were various opinions. Some temporarily took advantage of the situation and advocated a theory. Some adopted one-sided knowledge, regardless of whether it was suitable for the national conditions or not. Once a theory was formed, it was implemented as it was. There were also those who echoed others and touted each other to become supporters. Today, they introduce various foreign new theories without digesting them themselves, and want to implement them in China. There are few who do not think that today is right and yesterday was wrong, and few have seen results. The object of education is the people, and the people are not material, so they cannot be randomly given medicine for testing. To study which foreign education is applicable to China, we must first find out the boundary between theories and non-theories in this trend, which is the product of a kind of spirit and interest, and which is the cultural requirement produced by a combination of a kind of theory and reality. Then, we should consider the national conditions and set a standard so that it will be beneficial and harmless. However, this matter is of great importance, and we must gather talents from all over the country to cooperate in research and establish a center for Chinese education research. All those who return from studying abroad, after researching a certain subject, should implement it slowly, and do not rush to introduce it. They must undergo in-depth research and believe that it is in line and applicable before implementing it. Its research methods, such as "academic aspects," establish lecture groups, publication groups, and subject research groups. Lectures are for propaganda education and to supplement the education of teachers. There are two types: long-term and temporary. Publications are divided into annual reports, magazines, series, etc. Currently, each province, county, and education group publishes a publication. It seems that having a publication is good for appearance, but it is not economical. And most people who receive this kind of publication do not read it. If there is a central research institution, the materials will be rich in research, and the content will be exciting. Once published, many people will compete to read it. The circulation will be wide, and the effect will be seen naturally. "Artistic aspects" establish necessary equipment for painting education, handicraft education, and music drama. "Physical education aspects," such as sports physiology, use theoretical research to prove national skills. There are also the essentials of youth training, the methods and equipment of physical education. "Painting aspects" equip educational films and educational phantom films. "Equipment aspects," such as instruments, specimens, reference books, etc. in each subject classroom equipment, list the standard items that must be equipped for each subject and display them in one room, so that outside visitors can refer to and imitate them. Also, such as school buildings, educators, hygienists, and architects should be invited to jointly study an appropriate standard school building plan and separately set prices for those who build new school buildings in various places to imitate. (Russia divides the construction of school buildings into several types, such as those that can accommodate 200, 500, 800, and even 2,000 people. They are all stipulated separately. How to build and how much it costs to handle the procedure. If there is a construction, they will follow the procedure separately.) In addition, there must be exhibits available for research. The exhibits are divided into permanent, temporary, and roving types for observation. In short, educators themselves must have a sense of responsibility and cultivate students to have a sense of responsibility, creating the shoulders of the country that can bear all the national difficulties of China, not only bearing the current responsibility, but also having the responsibility for the future.

Ministry of Education Announces

Regulations for Studying Abroad

The Ministry of Education announced 46 regulations for studying abroad. The original text is as follows: Chapter 1 General Provisions

Article 1 All those who go abroad to study must follow the provisions of these regulations.

Article 2 Those who are admitted by the education administrative authorities of each province and city (hereinafter referred to as provinces and cities) or selected by public institutions to study specialized academic subjects abroad and are provided with all expenses during their study period are called public-funded students. All those who have their own funds to study abroad or are sent by private legal persons to study specialized academic subjects abroad and are provided with their expenses are called self-funded students.

Article 3 Each province and city shall set up scholarships for studying abroad under its education funds to encourage self-funded students from the province and city who have excellent achievements in studying abroad. The number of scholarships and methods shall be stipulated by each province and city and submitted to the Ministry for approval and implementation.

Article 4 If public and self-funded students have illegal behaviors, insult the country, or neglect their studies, the overseas student management institutions in the country where they are located may report to their original sending institutions or the Ministry to cancel their study qualifications and order them to return to the country. If they are public-funded students, they will also be required to return all the expenses they have previously received. Overseas student management institutions refer to overseas student supervision offices and embassies and consulates.

Chapter 2 Public-Funded Students

Article 5 Each province and city shall focus on specialized subjects such as agriculture, industry, medicine, and science when selecting and sending people to study specialized academic subjects abroad. The types of research subjects, the number of public-funded students, the countries to study in, the years of study, and the financial status shall be specified in detail by each province and city according to the needs of its local situation and the nature of the subjects to be studied before each enrollment and submitted to the Ministry for approval and implementation. However, the study period shall be at least two years and shall not exceed five years, including the internship and investigation periods.

Article 6 Public-funded students sent by each province and city shall be subject to the examination of each province and city and the re-examination of the Ministry. The aforementioned examination shall be held at most once a year in the same province and city. The registration date shall be from February 1st to March 1st. The examination date of each province and city shall be from April 1st to April 15th. The re-examination date of the Ministry shall be from July 1st to July 15th. Article 7 The detailed rules for the selection of public-funded students in each province and city shall be formulated by the education administrative authorities of each province and city in accordance with the provisions of these regulations and submitted to the Ministry for approval and implementation. The re-examination methods shall be determined separately by the Ministry.

Article 8 Those who have one of the following qualifications may register for the examination: (1) Graduates of public or registered private colleges or above at home and abroad, and have served in technical positions related to the subjects they have studied for more than two years; (2) After graduating from public or registered private colleges or above at home and abroad, they have continued to study the subjects they have studied for more than two years and have valuable specialized works or other achievements.

Article 9 When registering, in addition to submitting a graduation certificate and two recent 4-inch half-length photos (one to be kept by each province and city and one to be sent to the Ministry), those who have the qualifications mentioned in item 1 of the preceding article shall also submit two copies of a resume and a service certificate (one to be kept by each province and city and one to be sent to the Ministry). Those who have the qualifications mentioned in item 2 of the preceding article shall also submit specialized works or other achievements. The service certificate shall be signed and sealed by the head of the service institution.

Article 10 After the provincial and municipal authorities have reviewed the items in the preceding article and found them to be qualified, they may participate in the examination.

Article 11 The examination items are as follows: (1) Preliminary examination: (A) Physical examination. Those who fail the physical examination shall not participate in the B and C examinations. (B) General subjects: 1. Party doctrine, 2. Chinese language, 3. Chinese history and geography, 4. The language of the country to study in (composition, translation, conversation), (C) Specialized subjects. The specialized subjects shall be determined according to the subjects to be examined, but there must be at least five subjects. (2) Re-examination: (A) The language of the country to study in (composition, translation, conversation), (B) Specialized subjects. Two specialized subjects shall be selected from the specialized subjects of the preliminary examination. Those who are proficient in other foreign languages (excluding Japanese) but are less proficient in the language of the country to study in may replace it with other foreign languages, but after passing the re-examination, they must make up for the language of the country to study in at home. Those who pass the make-up examination at the second re-examination will be issued a formal re-examination passing certificate. The above-mentioned make-up examination is limited to once.

Article 12 The calculation of the preliminary examination results shall be: Party doctrine, Chinese language, and Chinese history and geography in the general subjects shall account for 25% of the total score, the language of the country to study in shall account for 25%, and the specialized subjects shall account for 50%. The re-examination results shall be calculated by averaging the three subjects.

Article 13 Those who pass the examination of the provincial and municipal authorities shall be given a preliminary examination passing certificate, and shall submit the examination results of the admitted students, together with the items mentioned in Article 9, to the Ministry for record before May 15. Those who pass the re-examination will be given a re-examination passing certificate, and those who fail the re-examination may not request another re-examination. The provincial and municipal authorities may admit twice the number of students to be sent for each subject for the preliminary examination and send them to the Ministry for re-examination (to be continued)

Local News

The Municipal Education Bureau Sends Personnel

To Beijing and Hangzhou to Negotiate Intelligence Tests

Since Director Pan took office in the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, he has devoted himself to the research of educational science. Four symptomatic solutions were proposed: (1) Finding ways to promote the sale of inventory; (2) Requesting national banks to provide low-interest loans; (3) Providing various transportation conveniences; (4) Shortening the period of reduced working hours and not reducing wages further. Items (1) and (2) are to be handled by the Ministries of Finance and Industry in the shortest possible time, and item (3) is to be handled by the Ministry of Railways. British Parliament Discusses

China's Boxer Indemnity

Comparison of British and American Indemnity Refunds

Reuters dispatch from London on the 1st: Baldwin made a statement in the House of Commons today regarding the Chinese Boxer Indemnity. Conservative Party member Miller stated that the British refund of the Boxer Indemnity is about five times greater than that refunded by the United States. The United States has a memorial in the form of Tsinghua University. Has Britain also had a similar memorial to represent the sacrifice of British taxpayers? Baldwin replied that Miller's comparison of the Boxer Indemnity refunds between Britain and the United States is incorrect. The United States refunded approximately $35,000,000 out of its total indemnity of $53,000,000, approximately 65.5%. As for Britain, its total indemnity was £16,500,000, and the amount refunded was £11,000,000, approximately 68%. The British refund is used to repair or build railways and other profitable enterprises in China and to establish a fund for future educational purposes. According to the Sino-British agreement and the bill passed by the British Parliament in 1931, the distribution of this fund is determined by the trustees. Although there is no memorial, the British government considers this to be the most practical way to benefit both countries. Conservative Party member Somerville asked if part of this fund would be transferred to the University of Hong Kong. Baldwin said he would answer this question later.

The Opening of Summer

— Zhanlu

The spring scenery is gone, but the national crisis has not gone, and it is advancing step by step with the god of summer! Mentioning the word "summer" evokes many feelings: China is called "Huaxia," but Huaxia has encountered bad luck and become a world of "barbarians corrupting China." Xia is the name of the first dynasty among the Three Dynasties. Thinking of Yu the Great's eight years of footprints establishing mountains and rivers, what a great achievement! Unexpectedly, the vast traces of Yu have become fragmented rivers and mountains! Also, Rehe, Luanyang, Beidaihe, and other places are all good places to spend the summer and escape the heat, but now they are unimaginable! Summer, oh summer, what are you here to do? With mixed feelings, I sing the opening of summer:

Ninety days of spring are gone and will not return, welcoming summer is also appropriate; The trivial thing is, being startled and experiencing scorching summer, let's talk about the word "summer" from the beginning: Anciently, Huaxia referred to China alone, Why is it that the barbarian's fortune prospers while Xia's declines? Only ending up with, barbarians corrupting China and entering the Yuguan pass! I remember, among the Three Dynasties of Shang and Zhou, there was Xia first, Yu the Great waded and established rivers and mountains: Today, who will recover the fragmented rivers and mountains? In the vast universe, enemies come again, We can only, cry mournfully on the tomb of King Xia! I also remember, the grand hall is called Xiawu, Helplessly, the swaying wind and rain have already collapsed; The swallows and sparrows in the hall are still not aware, Still, they go back and forth dancing in pavilions and singing on stages, How can they, in the backyard, forget to miss their homeland? Today, I fear reading the record of spending summer in Luanyang, Spending summer in Luanyang is always difficult; Beidaihe, suffers disasters, lamenting the ashes of the region for spending summer! Thinking of, finishing grieving for spring and regretting summer, old grudges and new sorrows cannot be dispelled, I can only, entrust the vastness of human affairs to the wine cup!

The Expression of Human Nature

— Xianxian

In the dance halls and gambling places of grand hotels, and in all social gatherings, regardless of men, women, old, or young, everyone has a golden expression, using snow-white silver dollars as if they were radish slices. In those places, the human instinct to love money is obscured. Some say that these things happen at night. Night is the time for humans to rest. Activity during rest time is fundamentally abnormal. An abnormal life naturally obscures human nature. If you want to see the expression of human nature, it is best to do so in the early morning. When you prop up your pillow and have had enough sleep, your mind is especially clear. That is the only time to reveal your true self.

These unanalyzed, and I don't know whether or not they align with philosophical, pedantic remarks have recently given me a very good impression. This is how it is. One morning, I went to the small vegetable market with my wife and children. By the green vegetable stall, I ran into a certain lady who I often see at the dog racing track but whose name I do not know. This certain lady buys tickets very ruthlessly, always spending twenty or thirty dollars at a time, and doesn't care about losing. But I saw her buying green vegetables, her face turned iron-green for the sake of a single coin, and she almost started a fight with the vegetable seller. In the end, the certain lady got a penny's worth of benefit, and as she left, she also grabbed a handful of free vegetables. This is the truest expression of human nature.

If readers are interested in sightseeing at the small vegetable market, they can certainly learn a very good lesson. In the small vegetable market, all kinds of disputes with bulging veins on the forehead, as thick as thumbs, are just over the difference of a single penny. This expression of human nature may seem somewhat undignified, but in fact, it makes a lot of sense. The big shots who give away sovereign territory to others are like the rich old men who only move around at night, seeing everything as relaxed and ordinary. Heroes who kill the enemy with great force are just like the sellers and buyers in the small vegetable market, showing a face that refuses to be taken advantage of everywhere.

The Wonderful Use of Rings

— Limin

We Chinese people have traditionally regarded rings as unnecessary decorations, without any implications. Later, after a generation of newly married couples who opposed the old moral teachings used rings as tokens of engagement, the ring became something with meaning. Because Princess Henry of England wore her wedding ring on the ring finger of her left hand when she married, it created a special custom, creating a worldwide habit. The following standards were discovered later:

The middle finger indicates the meaning of engagement.

The index finger indicates the meaning of proposing marriage.

The little finger indicates the ideal of celibacy.

Many women in the United States, in order to avoid the crush of marriage proposals, wear a wedding ring on their ring finger to reject the entanglements of men. Therefore, the sales of wedding rings in the United States each year amount to tens of millions.

The prostitutes in China use rings to indicate when they have their period, and they also use a ring to ward off clients from staying. This has the same meaning as marriage.

However, there are still many people who show off and do not know the meaning of rings, and often use them as decorations. This is too much of a letdown!

Lamenting Spring

— Drunken Fool

People are shouting, "Spring has arrived!" Who knew that the "God of Spring" seemed ashamed to show its face, still not gracing us with its presence. You think, since the beginning of spring, the spring cold has been lingering, the spring rain has been continuous, and everyone is calling out that they are cold. The days with warm wind, gentle breeze, and bright spring sunshine are simply very, very few. Although I want to deliberately seek out spring, I still have a sense that "spring scenery doesn't know where to go." Now it is "flowing water, fallen flowers, spring has gone." In the blink of an eye, ninety days of good spring are about to bid farewell to people. But spring, when gone, will come again someday; I don't know when the lost magnificent mountains and rivers can be returned? Facing this slanting wind and fine rain, looking north at the clouds and mist, I can't help but feel "spirit broken in sadness"!

Carrot Top's Whiskers

— Written by IULES RENARD, Translated by Lin Qu

Carrot Top's Whiskers found a mole on the road as black as a chimney sweep. After he had played with it enough, he decided to kill it. Several times he threw it into the sky, throwing it so skillfully that it landed precisely on a rock.

At first, the process went very well and was done very quickly.

The mole's legs were already broken, its skull had already been cracked open, and its back was also shattered. Its life didn't seem very sturdy. But then, Carrot Top's Whiskers saw that it wasn't completely dead, and this terrified him. Although he threw it very high, over the roof, into the sky, he could not find a way to kill it.

"This bastard! It's not dead yet," he cursed.

Indeed, on that blood-stained stone, the mole was a mangled mess; its fat belly trembled like congealed juice, and because of this trembling, it still seemed alive.

"It's awful!" Carrot Top's Whiskers became fanatical, he shouted: "It's not dead yet!"

He picked it up, cursing it, and changed his method.

His face flushed red with anger and tears welling up in his eyes, he spat on it, holding it very close, and threw it onto the stone with all his might. But that unsightly belly still trembled.

And, as Carrot Top's Whiskers frantically beat it even harder, the mole seemed even less dead.

***

Carrot Top's Whiskers and his older brother Felix hurried home after finishing their prayers, because it was four o'clock in the afternoon, time for a snack.

Older brother Felix could get a piece of bread spread with butter or jam, while Carrot Top's Whiskers could only get a piece of dry bread. This was because he wanted to act like a grown-up early on, and had declared in front of many people that he was not greedy. He liked simple things and usually ate dry bread with a serious air. This afternoon he walked faster than older brother Felix, wanting to be the first to get the bread.

Sometimes dry bread seemed very difficult to swallow. So Carrot Top's Whiskers, like attacking an enemy, used all his strength to grab it, biting it desperately with his teeth, breaking it into pieces, causing crumbs to fly everywhere. The people in his family stood around, watching him with great curiosity.

His ostrich-like stomach could digest even stones or copper-green ancient coins.

In short, he ate things in the most casual way possible.

He pressed the bolt on the door. The door was already locked.

"I think Mom and Dad are not at home. You kick it," he said.

Older brother Felix, cursing, vigorously slammed the heavy door studded with many nails for a long time, making it creak. Then the two of them worked together again, hitting the door with all their strength, injuring their shoulders, but the door still did not open.

"They must not be at home," Carrot Top's Whiskers said.

"Then where did they go?" Older brother Felix asked angrily.

"No one can know everything. Let's just sit down for a while."

They sat on the cold steps, feeling a rare hunger. Sometimes yawning, sometimes pounding their chests with their fists, expressing their anger.

Felix: If they think I'll wait for them, they're wrong!

Carrot Top's Whiskers: But if we don't wait, what can we do?

Felix: I really won't wait for them. I don't want to starve. I want to eat right now, whatever it is. Even grass will do.

Carrot Top's Whiskers: Eat grass! That's a good idea, then they'll be fooled.

Felix: Hey! People eat lettuce "SALADE" and they eat it very well. For example, if we eat alfalfa, isn't it as tasty as lettuce? It's lettuce without oil and vinegar. (To be continued)

Commercial News

Finance

Silver Futures Rebound by $1.50

Long-Term Silver Prices Fail to Satisfy Expectations

Western Merchants Frenziedly Purchase Spot Goods, Leading to Scarcity

Smelting Costs Rise to Over $50

After a decline the day before, the gold market rebounded yesterday. Various rumors had little significant impact. The foreign exchange market performed poorly, with banks restricting transactions and many traders covering short positions due to the inflated currency in the US, which increased paper money supply and devalued gold. The US dollar in the local market should have weakened, but the gold market was affected by the US gold ban, leading to a perceived cash shortage and unfavorable swap rates. As a result, gold prices stabilized, further squeezing hedging opportunities. Market sentiment was stable today. Early morning reports of rising US bank rates had little impact, with initial gains quickly met by profit-taking due to hardened domestic bank rates. However, prices soon rebounded. Western merchant Xiang Meng, acting through Shen Kang, purchased over a thousand bars, further drying up the spot market and stabilizing sentiment. Although unconfirmed rumors circulated, their impact was limited due to the positive market atmosphere. Flour and Wheat Have Slightly Tightened in the Past Two Days

The recent situation of flour is generally fluctuating steadily. A record of the past two days is written to clarify its trends. When the market opened on the first day, the prices of ocean wheat, both in Zhigan and elsewhere, rose by over 1 dollar each. But domestic buying power is weak, and the society is generally in an recession, so after the market opened, prices only rose by one or two cents, and there was no big rise. In the afternoon, because small factories gave their products at low prices, prices went back down by 1/10th to 1/100th of a dollar. The total volume of transactions in the whole city was only around 200,000 bags. When prices opened on the second day, the prices of ocean wheat went back down by 10-20 cents, and people were unsteady in their minds. But because factories did not want to sell, there was very little activity. However, the small traders did a bit of buying, so the atmosphere in the market seemed to be steady. This afternoon, prices did not decrease, but because there weren't a lot of people selling, and some people who were outside the market still wanted to buy, the price of futures went slightly higher. Overall, compared to the closing price last month, this month's price is higher by 7.5/1000 of a cent, June's price is higher by 1.5/100 of a cent, July's price is higher by 1.75/100 of a cent, August's price is higher by 1.25/100 of a cent, September's price is higher by 7.5/1000 of a cent, and October's market opened at 2 dollars, 4 cents, and 9.5/100 of a cent, which is less by 1.2/100 of a cent.

For the situation in wheat futures on days one and two, things were generally smooth. Though the prices of wheat in the ocean rose sharply in the market on day one, today's factories already have a lot of wheat on hand, and so they don't want to buy any wheat for the standards, so the market didn't go very high. When the market opened yesterday, wheat had already gone down by 10-20 cents, but there weren't a lot of people who wanted to get rid of their wheat, and both sides were observing, so there was very little trading, and prices were slightly tight. Judging from this kind of situation, it will only be possible to enter a bustling situation after a new stock comes out. As a result, July's price was 6/100 of a cent higher than last month's closing price, and August's and September's prices were 4/100 of a cent higher.

Chinese Park

— Zhao Ziming

Although the Bund Park has trees, flowers, rockeries... its location along the riverbank makes it hazy and lacking elegance. It doesn't compare to the verdant forests and clear ponds of the Zhaofeng Park, where every part blends naturally. If one steps into the Chinese Park by the Suzhou Creek, one realizes it's not even up to par with the Bund Park. Compared to Zhaofeng Park, it's like a small witch in the presence of a great one.

The Chinese Park is indeed for the common people; no ticket is required for admission. Near the entrance is a restroom, reeking with a foul odor. The walls are plastered with advertisements for "curing spermatorrhea," "accurate psychic readings," "herbs for menstruation," and "treating syphilis".... a dazzling array, beautifully presented. Next to the restroom are food stalls selling cigarettes, peanuts, pancakes, fried dough sticks..., where rickshaw pullers gather to feast, relishing the flavors.

Now in springtime, the park's lawns remain barren, and the leaves on the trees are still withered, resembling a deep autumn plain. The open space is filled with many birdcages. Leisurely Suzhou residents, holding cigarette holders, enthusiastically pit their birds against each other. Songbirds are their second life. What state has the nation reached? How painful is it to be a conquered and enslaved people?... They will never think about it. It's truly a case of "No sorrow is greater than the death of the heart." Alas, what more can be said?

To the west of the park is a thatched pavilion. A young mistress reclines on a bench, singing whatever comes to mind: "A horse leaves the western Liang border..." A dirty-faced child jumps on the bench, laughing, smiling, and crying... The ground is covered in phlegm, peanut shells, and cigarette butts, an utter mess. Where is the Chinese people's sense of morality? No wonder foreign parks previously restricted Chinese people from entering.

The Chinese Park hardly deserves to be called a "park"; it's just a gathering place for hooligans and mistresses!

Qing Society Rehearsal Report: The Qing Society Opera Troupe rehearsed at the Lake Society yesterday. The program was filled with excellent performances, a feast for the eyes. The highlight was undoubtedly "Kneeling by the Pond," where the three actors collaborated seamlessly from beginning to end. The tightness of their coordination and the realism of their expressions were truly remarkable, a rare feat among opera enthusiasts. Next was "Parting from Mother to Return to Camp," which was both energetic and poignantly tragic, and "Portraying an Experienced Hand," which showcased amazing skill and charm, deserving of special recognition. "Jiao Cu Drunk Yuan" was a masterpiece by a famous artist, truly extraordinary, with the bursts of laughter being particularly unique. "Night Lesson Dream" juxtaposed sorrow and joy perfectly, while "Flirting with the Qin and Stealing Poetry" was delicate, touching, and moving. "Small Banquet at Broken Bridge" was skillfully coordinated, a perfect combination. "Visiting the Broadsword Society" was powerful and grand, a rare achievement. "Longing for the Mortal World" and "Auspicious Day" were light and fluid, while "Debating Swords and Sending a Son" was generous and stirring, each displaying its own strengths. "Looking in the Mirror and Feeding Horses" was extremely comical, bringing everyone to laughter. With such excellent productions, it's no wonder opera lovers watch day and night, with doubled enthusiasm. (Wang Qi)

Social Sketches

Comedy

— Lin Zichun

In order to visit a friend in H City to discuss some matters, I had to take another Yangtze River steamer.

In the cabin across from mine, there was a modern and fit young woman. Perhaps because there were few passengers, she, like me, occupied a cabin alone. Her door was often open, and those passing by could see clearly that she was always lying in bed reading. Except for the "toilet" issue, she rarely left her room, even eating her meals inside.

A young man in a suit, I don't know if he was a passenger, lingered most enthusiastically at her cabin door, constantly humming the song that Macdonald and Jeanette MacDonald sang in the movie "The Merry Widow." His walking and whistling were quite impressive, causing other passengers to shake their heads in admiration.

The next day, after dinner, I felt bored and went to the ship's purser's office to chat with the staff. We were acquainted, so the conversation was relaxed. We had been talking for a while when the modern young woman suddenly came into the purser's office.

"Are you the purser?" she asked politely.

"Yes, Madam. Is there anything we can assist you with?" the staff replied. "It's outrageous! There is a young man in a suit who is always walking back and forth in front of my cabin door and winking at me! I ignored him. Originally, I left my cabin door open because the air in the room was not very good. To avoid this man, I had to close the door. Unexpectedly, he then looked through the window. Tonight, he even wrote this note to me. Take a look." As she spoke, she handed a note written in pencil to a Mr. X on the staff.

"...You are an angel from heaven, and I admire you immensely. But you always ignore me! ...I feel there is nothing left for me in this world! I have decided to drown myself tonight at X hour. ...The luggage I leave behind in cabin X, please kindly deliver to my family. I am eternally grateful..."

X.X. Sincerely

(Date)

The handwriting on the note was not good, and there were a few typos! The above is what I wrote based on his meaning.

"Ah... a joke, a joke! Does one have to send out invitations before committing suicide? He seems to be saying, (Respectfully request your presence at the suicide of X.X. on X month X day at X hour.) What a joke, a strange story! Madam, please go back to sleep peacefully. Don't be afraid, we'll take care of everything," a member of the staff said, reassuring her after reading the note.

"Hey... the time has come, go ask him," Mr. X said to the tea servers. Immediately, several tea servers stepped forward and grabbed the young man. Then I and the staff also stepped forward.

"Sir... are you a guest in cabin X?... You are young and have a bright future... Why do you want to commit suicide?... Our country is facing such great difficulties! Isn't sacrificing yourself for the country more honorable than this meaningless suicide?" the staff members said noisily to the young man.

"I am not committing suicide, why are you grabbing me?... " The young man seemed to realize that his ruse had been exposed, and his speech was somewhat unnatural. "Didn't you tell the female guest in cabin X that you were going to drown yourself? And... here is the note you gave to that female guest," the staff countered.

The noisy commotion alarmed many passengers, who came running out to see what was happening. The young woman was also among them, and pointed at the young man, saying, "It's him. Is this person crazy?" A middle-aged guest in his thirties said.

"No... perhaps a drowned ghost has possessed him? Quickly, slap him on the face a few times, and you can scare away the drowned ghost," an old woman among the passengers said.

The young man tried to break free from the tea servers' grip and explain that he was not committing suicide... A tea server had already slapped him on the face several times before releasing him from the crowd, with a "reddened" face.

This comedy ended with everyone "Hahaha..." as if they were very satisfied with the show.

Free Talk

"Claiming to be Nanyang Ge, People Remember Qin Hui"

— Cao Juren

Recently, someone in Beiping wrote a humorous poem: "Claiming to be Nanyang Ge, People Remember Qin Hui." One sentence exposes the secret in the hearts of some people today!

"Zhuge's great name is known throughout the universe," isn't this the best thing in the world? Unfortunately, "great name" is not the same as garbage, which can be picked up everywhere. When Zhuge Liang descended from Wolong Ridge, it was when Liu Bei was destined to decline. Given Liu Bei's past friendship with Cao Cao, Zhuge Liang could have done a favor and advised Liu Bei to surrender to Cao Cao, securing a lifetime of wealth. But Zhuge did not do this. He had to personally seek help from General Sun and fight Cao Cao to the death. Liu Bei was defeated at Guoting, and "died midway" in Baidicheng. According to the principle of "internal stability before external resistance," Zhuge Liang should have first fought Sun Wu to the death before embarking on his six expeditions to Qishan. But Zhuge, entrusted with the heavy responsibility of guardianship, first reconciled with Sun Wu, determined that "Han and the rebel cannot coexist," and that "six expeditions to Qishan" were necessary. With Zhuge Liang's reputation and status, if he had secretly reconciled with Sima Yi, why wouldn't he have "wealth forced upon him"? But he "exhausted his efforts" until his death in Wuzhangyuan, still insisting that "Han and the rebel cannot coexist," and ordered Jiang Wei to carry on his legacy. Such a great name, known throughout the universe, was obtained with too much hardship. Are there any such Zhuge Liang today?

In front of Yue Fei's tomb, there is a couplet by a certain lady, the second line being "White iron innocently cast treacherous officials." Qin Hui probably didn't care about such posthumous matters. At the time, Hui wanted to obtain the position of Prime Minister, declaring, "I have two strategies that can stir the world." After he became Prime Minister, he indeed presented two strategies: "Returning the people of Hebei to Jin, returning the people of the Central Plains to Liu Yu." He decided on the grand plan of peace talks, telling Gaozong, "Officials are fearful and hesitant, mostly holding two opinions. This is not enough to discuss major matters. If Your Majesty is determined to make peace, please discuss it exclusively with me and do not allow the officials to participate." When the officials opposed the peace talks, Hui angrily said, "Hui only desires to benefit the country!" So direct and straightforward, wanting peace, then peace. No matter how you laugh or scold, he wouldn't care. He killed Yue Fei, and after his death, knelt in front of Yue Fei's tomb, allowing thousands of people to defile him. He was perfectly willing. I wonder if anyone is learning from Qin Hui today?

The poem says: "Shouldering the universe with one pole, it's easy to lift but hard to put down. I advise you to hold it high with a sky-supporting hand, many bystanders watch with cold eyes!" I would like to recite this poem again!

Visiting the Sick

— Qiu Peng

Pushing open the door, the gatekeeper's gloomy face emerged from beside the gate bar.

"?"

"Ward 420?"

"Upstairs," the gatekeeper raised a hand and casually waved it to the left, showing not only indifference but also some weariness.

I followed the direction he waved me in, my feet so heavy, dragging step by step! Turning the corner, I saw the white terrazzo staircase winding like a snake ahead. On both sides were white walls and white curtains; a nurse in white slowly pushed a two-wheeled cart, which contained a patient covered in a white sheet, a deathly white face... I followed the staircase, countless white circles flashing before my eyes, an eerie, underworld-like feeling invading my heart, I drifted like a ghost!

"NO 420" Suddenly this number clearly jumped before my eyes, so I gently knocked on the door with this number nailed on it. A middle-aged woman with swollen eyes opened the door for me, letting me in before gently closing it again. Dragging behind the woman was a skinny child of about five or six years old, who was staring at me with wide eyes. On the hospital bed by the window, Mr. XX lay still like a corpse, his deeply sunken eyes slightly closed, a few sparse, pale hairs scattered like withered grass on his dry head... As I approached his bedside, he opened his absent eyes and stared at me for a while before extending a withered hand and beckoning me to sit on the edge of the bed.

"Feeling better?" I began awkwardly with condolences:

"It's just a matter of time, there's no hope of survival."

"What's wrong?" My tone of surprise was overly strong.

"Tuberculosis! The doctor said the disease is entirely due to long-term overwork without adequate rest, especially since it shouldn't have been delayed until half of the lung has been eroded by mold! It's all too late... This, how could I not know? But XX, you tell me, in an environment like mine, is there an opportunity for me to rest? Every time I endure the hidden pain in my chest and work, I think, isn't this accelerating the destruction of my remaining life? So, let go! But I can't ignore my wife and children's food and clothing! Struggling like this until today, who knew it would finally be this..."

He choked up and turned his face away, two tears streaming from his deeply sunken eyes.

A heavy sorrow pressed down on my heart; I sat silently.

"Actually, 'death' seems as ordinary to me as sleeping. What is there to be nostalgic about in a life like mine? The suffering is for those two, the mother and child. How will they be in the future..."

He stopped his tears and raised his dim eyes to look at his wife, who was burying her face in her handkerchief, sobbing; the child looked at his dad, then at his mom, and suddenly grabbed his mom's sleeve and burst into tears.

He closed his eyes and turned his face away again!

"Another result of long-term labor exploitation!" I suddenly closed my eyes as well.

American Family Life

— Qian Gechuan

When material civilization reaches a certain level, the structure of society will also change. Whether the family can continue to exist forever will become a problem. Modern American family life shows us just such a meaning. Because of the development of machinery in America, individuals have extra time, and because of complete equipment, household labor is almost unnecessary, coupled with the bankruptcy of chastity, male-female relationships have no guarantee to speak of. So although there is the form of a family, there is no reality of a family. This kind of family that is insecure from morning to evening is really worthy of sociologists to study. The form of human life is originally the factor that determines social organization, and modern mechanical life has launched a great revolution against the basic family of human life. Modern Americans, benefiting from mechanical civilization, have almost only one-tenth of the work left in the home compared to the past. Everything needed in the family does not require manual labor to obtain. Water can be brought by tap water pipes, fire can be supplied by gas and electricity, and boiling water is boiling in the basement from morning to night. The housewife only needs to use her slender hands to turn the faucet, and then there is water, there is fire. Sitting at home without moving, it is not only possible to have boiling water, but it is also easy to have ice in hot weather. Because there is a kind of electric ice maker, you only need to put cold water in it, and it can turn into ice. With gas and electricity, boiling water and cold ice are all available. As you can see, it is not very laborious to cook. However, those living a family life in America are unwilling to do even this little bit of trouble. When they are hungry, they gently pick up the phone and make a call, and in less than a quarter of an hour, a sumptuous banquet is displayed in front of them. The only place of happiness is no longer the family in modern America. They are really at home too little. Except for breakfast, ordinary families eat out.

Modern American buildings have doors and windows that can fit together perfectly, with no gaps, and dust from the outside is not easy to enter. Moreover, they have a kind of vacuum cleaner, which sucks up all the dust and debris when pushed around the room. The beds are installed in wall cabinets, turned to the middle of the room at night, and then put away in the morning.

The thing that can best maintain a family is children, but modern American women are mostly unwilling to give birth to children. Even if they have them, infants can be sent to hospitals, and when they grow up a little, they can still be entrusted to nurses or specially hired nannies to take care of them. Mothers without money have to come out to work during the day, and children are also sent to day care centers for foster care. (After the children reach adulthood, they treat their parents like strangers.)

Even housewives are like this in the family, not to mention men. The place where the family has a relationship with them is only sleeping at night and receiving letters in the morning. So they don't need an independent family, and many people use apartments or hotels as permanent residences. Because there, even the equipment in the family and the trouble of turning on the faucet are unnecessary. Since the family is already unnecessary and no one needs to be taken care of, of course both men and women have the extra energy to develop outwards. Modern American women can enter the Presidential Palace as cabinet members and go abroad as ambassadors. Women who only talk about sitting at home as housewives, like Chinese women, are of course very few. Men and women have to go out to work during the day and cannot stay together all day long, so the so-called family reunion happiness is naturally greatly reduced. Since women do not rely on men economically, they can be free. They are now unwilling to continue to abide by the kind of chastity that only forced women to abide by in the past. What is divorce? A woman does not become unmarriageable because of one divorce. Moreover, after a divorce, men usually have to pay alimony, so women always get the advantage, so most divorces in America are initiated by women. Today, it seems that there is one divorce out of every five marriages in America. Today, let's browse American literary news THE (To be continued)

Zhang Xueliang Visits Gandhi

— Wu

My goodness! Ships and trains really do run too fast. The buzzing of Comrade Zhang's "resignation" and "going abroad" is still fresh in our ears, but now, in the blink of an eye, he has arrived in Bombay, India. It is said that when Tang Sanzang went to the Western Paradise to obtain scriptures, even though he rode a white horse that was the embodiment of a divine dragon, it still took him many years, and he might not even have been to Bombay. So, scientific inventions are truly too convenient for people like our Comrade Zhang to "resign" and "go abroad," or to go abroad for recuperation. This is something we ordinary people wouldn't even dare to dream of.

Comrade Zhang Xueliang's trip abroad has really been a breath of fresh air, and he has even resolved to give up his habits. Some people say that this is because European and American countries have not implemented "opium monopolies," which would be very inconvenient. But in reality, he wants to sincerely be a model Chinese person to win honor for China. Precisely for this reason, of course, he must also promote non-resistance to the fullest extent, to "correct international perception." So, in Bombay, he decided to visit his teacher, Gandhi. Unfortunately, he was not granted permission by the government and had to abandon the idea.

However, we can fully believe that Comrade Zhang will "continue to work hard to implement" this great doctrine. His teacher, the sage Gandhi, will certainly do the same. Although one is in the wilderness, one is in prison, one is a citizen of a subjugated nation, and one is a promising general of a nation on the verge of subjugation, their endeavors are all successful. The facts are before our eyes. In recent years, many toiling masses in India have gloriously sacrificed themselves for this great doctrine, and China's achievements are even more remarkable, astounding foreigners. If the British government were to "permit" him to meet Gandhi, reaching out their hands through iron bars, then one would call out "Brother," and the other would call out "Worthy Brother," and everyone would smile knowingly, all understanding each other without words. The most regrettable thing is that the British government will certainly not allow him to visit. Otherwise, if the teacher and disciple could meet, and from then on work even harder, the doctrine would become popular, and all the weak and small nations of the world would, under the command of non-resistance, allow imperialism to conquer them with peace of mind. And these two teachers and disciples would thus enjoy high official positions and salaries, and enjoy peace and prosperity.

Another point is that our Comrade Zhang's leisure and elegance at this moment are also most obvious. The reason is that Bombay is so far away from Nanjing, and Nanjing is also far away from the outside of the Great Wall. Of course, the sounds of imperialist cannons cannot be heard. Even if they immediately attack Tianjin and Beiping, it would not necessarily be detrimental to our comrades. Therefore, we can confidently predict that the doctrine of non-resistance will surely be passed down from generation to generation. However, Gandhi's non-resistance and Zhang Xueliang's non-resistance are actually somewhat different.
